# DFS : Finding Max Height of a  Binary Tree

```cpp
int maxDepth(TreeNode* root) {
            if (!root) return 0;
            int left = maxDepth(root->left);
            int right = maxDepth(root->right);

            return 1 + max(left, right);
        }
```

Depth Fist Search (DFS) : Finding max Height ^SxyxgiJW

Check if a binary tree is balanced ^l7sxfuGe

Maximum Difference between
left sub tree and right subtree should be 
at most 1 ^q3YcARZ6

This is helpful in propagating 
back once one of the node is 
found to be unbalnaced ^ua68n54m

Check if a binary tree is balanced ^v1YiSOWN

algo:
for each node in main tree do dfs with subtree


dfsMain(node *root)
if(node == nullptr) return 0;

dfsMain(root->left);
if (childDfs(root, subroot)) return 1;
dfsMain(root->right);

return false;


childdfs(node, subroot)



childdfs(node* p, node*c):
if(p == nullptr && c == nullptr) return true;

if (p == nullptr || c == nulptr) return false;

if(p->val == q->val):
    return childdfs(p->left, q->left) && childdfs(p->right, q->right);

return false; ^teVOWnxE
